 police kii koshish he ki kisi tarah aropiyon ko dhundha jaae

 sisitivi kii tasveeron main commered pansre or unki patni ke baad, do bike savaar dikh rahe hai

 Pune SIT chief Sanjeev Kumar said, "the accused are seen in the footage, but the picture is not very clear
" 
 
 jo sketch or footage hamane jari kiya he usase hamen ummid he ki aaropee jald pakade jaaenge

 tippaniyan Comrade Pansare and his wife were shot dead by unidentified assailants while returning from Morning Walk on the day of February 16, 2015

 He was a known satirist of the country
 raajnneetik vishaya par unki adbhut pakad thi
 Parsai chose freelance writing as a way of life, leaving the temptation of any kind of job

 Apart from these, Parsai also wrote stories, novels and essays
 unki kritiyon main upanyaas- rani naagfani kii kahani, tat kii khoj, jwaala or jal; kahani-sangrah- hanste hai rote hai, jaise unke din phire; vyangy niabandh sangrah- tab kii baat or thi, bhoot ke paanv peeche, beyimaani kii parat, vaishnav kii phislan, ‘pagadendion kaa jamaana, shikaayat mujhe bhi he, sadachaar kaa taabeej, premchand ke fate juute, aawaara bheed ke khatre, sadachaar kaa taabeej, apni apni beemaari, do naak vaale log, kaag bhagoda, maati kahe kumhaar se, aisa bhi sochaa jaataa he, viklang shraddha kaa daur, tirchhi rekhaayen or sansmornatmak niabandh- ham ek umr se waakif hai, jane pahachaane log shaamil he
 The specialty of Harishankar Parsai's writing is that he does not write only for humor or humor
 unka sara lekhan soddeshy he or sabhi rachanaaon ke peeche ek saaf-sulajhi hui vaigyanik jivan-drushti he, jo samaaj main faile hue bhrashtachar, dhong, avasarvadita, andhvishwaas, sampradayikta aadi kupravritiyon par tej roshni daalane ke liye har samay satark rahati he
 No matter how light-hearted they are, but every essay provides an insight to understand the complex situation of today

 yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he) Uttarakhand Chief Minister Trivendra Singh Rawat released the latest figures for 2016-17 of census of tigers in Corbett and Rajaji Tiger Reserve
 corbett tigar rigerv main nunatam 208 vishisht baagh or rajaji tiger rigerv main nunatam 34 vishisht baaghon kii pahchaan kii gai he
 Last year, this number was found to be 163 in Corbett Tiger Reserve and 16 in Rajaji Tiger Reserve
 mukhyamantri ne kaha ki 340 baaghon ke saath kshetrafal ke anupaat main baaghon kii sankhya ke maamle main uttrakhand desh kaa nambar ek rajya ho gaya he
 However, Karnataka still ranks first with 400 tigers
 corbett tiger rigerv main lagaaye the 535 camerecorbett tiger rigerv kii sabhi renjo main grid ke aadhaar par camere lagaae gaye the
 Approximately 535 cameras were installed to count the tigers
 corbett tiger rigerv main baaghon kii ginati do charnon main kii gai
 The first phase was calculated from November 28, 2016 to January 21, 2017 at the Ramnagar Tiger Reserve Division of Corbett Tiger Reserve via the camera trap method
 vahiin duusare charan main dinaank 25 janvari, 2017 se dinaank 19 march, 2017 tak kalagarh tiger rigerv prabhag main camere ke madhyam se kii gai
 Two cameras were placed at each camera point
 ramnagar tigar rigerv main 235 camere ke point banaae gaye or camere 55 55 dinon ke liye lagaae gaye
 At the Kalagarh Tiger Reserve, cameras were installed for 54 days at 232 camera points
 is prakaar corbett tiger rigerv kii kul 25,453 trep nit se 4,24,870 photo mili
 a total of 3892 photographs of tigers were found in them
 baaghon kii ginati ke liye 2,539 tasviren istemaal huin
 The tigers were counted and the left and right parts of the picture were matched
 jisamen 142 vishisht baaghon ke baayen tathaa daaen pahalu (flank) mili
 Only left aspects of 66 distinct tigers were obtained
 baaghon kii ginatibaayen pahalu kaa aadhaar maanakar kii gai he
 96 tigers received right sides
 inkaa milan nahin kiya gaya tathaa inhen ginati main shaamil nahin kiya gaya
 Under the Corbett Tiger Reserve, 99 distinct tigers and 06 specialized cubs were identified in Ramnagar Tiger Reserve Division and 109 specific tigers were identified in Kalagarh Tiger Reserve Division
 is prakaar corbett tiger rigerv main baagh gananaa phej-4 2016-17 kii gananaa main nunatam 208 vishisht baaghon va 06 vishisht shavakon kii pahchaan kii gai he
 In the year 2015, this number was found to be 163 in phase-iv
 rajaji tiger rigerv main bhi sthiti shandarrajaji tiger rigerv main bhartiya vanyajeev santhaan va vishwa prakruti nidhi (dablyoo

 epa
 ) Phase-4 monitoring was done in the year 2016-17
 ek camera trep kaa ghanatv 1
 5 square kilometers were laid
 rigerv ke kor kshetra main 562 camere upyog main laae gaye
 This work was done from January 28, 2017 to June 03, 2017 in 10 ranges of core area
 prayek range main 25-30 raaton ko camere lagaate huye kul 15,330 trep nits main 620 baaghon kii photo praapt hui
 Specific tigers were identified by analyzing them
 rajaji tiger rigerv ke antargat nunatam 34 vishisht baaghon tathaa 05 vishisht shavakon kii pahchaan kii gai

 party upaadhyaksh shanta kumaar ne kaha, ‘videshi bainkon main bharat ke beyimaan logon dwaara chhipaakar rakhaa gaya dhan desh main waapas laayaa janaa chahie

 ’kumaar ne is baat par afsos prakat kiya ki paanch saal se bhrashtachar ke khilaaf sanyukt raashtra sandhipatr kaa hastaksharkarta hone ke baad bhi bharat ne abtak ise anumodith nahin kiya he

 bhaajapa upaadhyaksh ne kaha unhone pradhanmantri ko patr bhejkar kaha tha ki, ‘yadi ham kaale dhan ko waapas laane ke prati gambhirtha dikhaate hai to sweetrajraland madad karegaa lekin abtak mujhe us patr kaa jawaab nahin mila
 ' bhartiya samaaj kii mul bhaavana ahimsa, karunaa, aparigrih or aapas main bhaichaare kii he
 When these qualities are mentioned in a religious context, then the greatest Jain religion appears to be their greatest refuge
 lekin pichley saal 1 janvari ko jab gujarat ke junagarh jile main jainon ke param pavitra tirthasthal girnaar main muni prabal sagar par pranaghatak hamalaa hua to puure desh ke anya sahishnu logon kii tarah hi jain dharm ke log bhi sakate main aa gaye
 The attack took place in the state of Gujarat where the Chief Minister is already known for his religious fanaticism and bitter attitude towards minorities
 or desh ke is rajya main to jain samaaj ko alpsankhyak kaa darja bhi hasil nahin tha
 In such a situation, the central government was not able to help them much
 isi tarah lakhanu main saream hamaare aradhy tirthankar kii murti kaa bhanjan ki yaa gaya
 Here, theft of idols from temples and attacks on Jain saints also continued
 jain samaaj ke chaaron ang digambar, shwetambar, sthandwasi or terapanthi ke dharmik rahanuma in paristhitiyon se vikal ho gaye or unhen laga ki dharm kii raksha, aasthaa kaa nirvaah or muniyon kii suraksha ke liye jain samaaj ko alpsankhyak kaa darja dilaanaa jaruri he
 As seriously as the Jain society was feeling this pain, Congress President Sonia Gandhi, Rahul Gandhi and Hon'ble Prime Minister Manmohan Singh also understood it with great respect
 gandhi parivaar hameshaa se hi jain dharm ko lekar anuraagi rahaa he chaahe ve pratham pradhanmantri pandit ji hon yaa desh kii louh mahila indira gandhi
 The intention of the present leadership can be understood by my own example
 jain samaaj ko centre sarkaar main pratinidhitiv dene ke liye mere jaisaa adana-sa kaaryakarta, jo pehali baar saansad bana ho, ko centre sarkaar main mantri kii haisiyat se jagah di gai
 From time to time, the top people of Jain society met Rahul Gandhi and sent to him that the right time had come to give minority status to Jain society
 rahul gandhi kii sahmati ke baad alpsankhyak maamalon ke tatkaaleen mantri salmaan khurshid or vartmaan mantri ke
 Law Minister Kapil Sibal, along with Rehman Khan, worked very hard to put this proposal in the cabinet accurately
 iske liye main vyaktigat rup se unka bahut abhaari hum
 i and the Jain society know that the status of Jain society will not change overnight just by getting legal status
 lekin ab samaaj ke paas kam-se-kam apni baat rakhane ke kanoonee vikalp honge
 If under the rule of an anti-minority leader like Narendra Modi, the prodigals would dare to repeat the Girnar-like scandal, then at least they can be brought to the forefront of the Minorities Commission
 jahaan tak canibet ke is nattejey ke vyaavhaarik asar kii baat he to jain samaaj na to naukariyon main aarakshan maang rahaa he or na alpsankhyak darja jaisi koi baat karata he
 That is, Jain society does not want even a full scope to kill the right of any religious society
 yah darja milane se jo khaas sahuliyatein jain samaaj ko milengi-masalan, isse jain samudaay kii suraksha badhegi
 Just as other minority religions impart their religious education through their schools, now Jain society will also be able to do that work
 is samudaay ke zyaadaatar log nijee vyavsaay se jude hai, aise main kam byaaj par lone or sasti takanic or vyavsaayik shiksha kii suvidha unhen bhi muhaiyaa ho jaaegi
 The biggest thing is that 50 percent seats will be reserved for Jain children in Jain colleges
 jain dharmavalambiyon ke dharmik sthal, sansthaaon, mandiron, tirth kshetron or trust kaa sarkarikaran yaa adhigrahan aadi nahin kiya ja sakegaa, balki dharmik sthalon kaa samuchit vikaas or suraksha ke vyapak prabandh shashan dwaara bhi kiye jaaenge
 Under the Place of Worship Act 1991 (42AA-18-9-91), there will be clear instructions for maintaining any place of religious worship, which is a crime punishable under Section 6 (3)
 samudaay dwaara sanchalit treston kii sampatti ko kiraaya niyantran adhinium se bhi mukt rakhaa jayega
 The responsibility of managing Jain temples, pilgrimage sites, educational institutions etc
 will be given in the hands of the community
 sarkaar jain samudaay ko skool, college, chatravaas, shodh yaa prashikshan santhaan kholane ke liye sabhi suvidhaayen or riyayati dar par jameen uplabdh karavaaegi
 Even more important is that the institutions run by the Jain community, which have been occupied by the majority under the guise of law, will be liberated
 jain dharmavalambee dwaara punearth, praani seva, shiksha ityadi ke liye daan dhan kar mukt hoga
 All this was also necessary because members of the Jain community reside in every state of the country except Lakshadweep
 jainon kii sankhya desh kii kul sankhya kaa maatr 0
 4 percent
 sarkari manyata se kahin pehle desh kii adaalatein jain samudaay kii is bhaavana par muhar lagaati rahi hai
 Actually, all the trouble started from 1992
 centre sarkaar dwaara nirmit rashtriya alpsankhyak ayog kanoon 1992 ke antargat 23 aktubar, 1993 ko ek notification jari kar muslim, isai, sikh, buddha evam parsi samaaj ko dharmik alpsankhyak samaaj ghoshit kiya gaya
 But Jain society was excluded from this list, whereas from 1973 to 1992 Jain society had this status
 centre sarkaar ke vartmaan faisle se pehle bhi chhattisgarh, rajasthan, haryana, dilli, uttar pradesh, madhya pradesh, karnataka, maharashtra, andhra pradesh, pashchim bengal, uttarakhand or jharkhand main jainon ko rajyastareey dharmik alpsankhyak samaaj kaa darja hasil tha
 Anyway, the way communal powers are raising their heads in the country, we should not forget the period of history when all religions played a role in nation building
 jain samaaj ne hameshaa se puure desh main dharmashalaayein or vishaal mandiron kaa nirmaan karaayaa
 The rich people of Jain society have always been making efforts to provide health services to all sections
 ab unke treston ko alpsankhyak kaa darja milane se yah kaam vyapak str par hoga
 We do not have enough numbers so that we can elect sufficient number of mlas or mps of our society, who in due time can make necessary laws to protect the traditions, dignities and interests of the society
 aarthik sampannataa ke is daur main dhanapati kaum kaa vah gaurav bhi aaj hamaare paas nahin he, jo kabhi hua k rata tha
 How many Jains are in the list of the wealthiest people of the country and at what number they are, it is well known
 yadi aaj bhi jain samaaj seva, udyog, vyapaar, shiksha, sanskaar ityadi kaary main sakriy he, to vah apane sanskaron ke kaaran he
 It is in the blood of the Jains that the more efforts they put into their lives, the more strong the feeling of being helpful to others, because our ideal is - "live and let live
" ’’aaj rahul gandhi kii manshaa se jain samaaj ko uskaa kanoonee haq mil gaya he
 But with this decision, the responsibility of Jain community has also increased
 hamen hameshaa dhyaan rakhana hoga ki bharat sabakaa he or jab koi samudaay vishesh apni sthiti ko zyada joardaar dhang se duusare samudaay par thopata he to saamaajik taane-bane main asantulan paidaa hota he
 Jain society has always been non-violent and it will have to fight its rights in the future
